<h2 class="kt-adv-heading18047_c76cce-2c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading18047_c76cce-2c"><strong>I’m Christina! A curly-haired 32-year-old from the UK.</strong></h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading18047_4cf1d0-4c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading18047_4cf1d0-4c">For the last 14 years, I’ve been absolutely hooked on travelling! It’s been a huge part of my life, and I’m particularly passionate about encouraging women to go out and explore the world (especially solo).<br><br>Whether it’s diving headfirst into the digital nomad lifestyle or squeezing in adventures around a regular job, I’ve done it all. Even travelling solo long-term while in a relationship!<br><br>So, if you’re after some travel inspo or need tips and tricks for your next adventure, you’re in the right place.</p>
